-> issues/NNS (root)
  -> It/PRP (nsubj)
  -> is/VBZ (cop)
  -> not/RB (neg)
  -> just/RB (advmod)
  -> human/JJ (amod)
  -> rights/NNS (compound)
  -> countries/NNS (nmod:in)
    -> in/IN (case)
    -> have/VBP (acl:relcl)
      -> which/WDT (nsubj)
      -> record/NN (dobj)
        -> a/DT (det)
        -> track/NN (compound)
        -> restricting/VBG (acl)
          -> of/IN (mark)
          -> published/VBN (ccomp)
            -> what/WP (nsubjpass)
            -> is/VBZ (auxpass)
            -> media/NNS (nmod:in)
              -> in/IN (case)
              -> the/DT (det)
              -> concern/NN (acl:relcl)
                -> that/WDT (nsubj)
                -> is/VBZ (cop)
                -> of/IN (case)
                -> bloggers/NNS (nmod:to)
                  -> to/TO (case)
  -> ./. (punct)
